<script>
      $.asm = {};
      $.asm.panels = 1;
      $('#toggleSidebar').click(function() {
        if ($.asm.panels === 1) {
          $('#toggleSidebar i').addClass('glyphicon-chevron-left');
          $('#toggleSidebar i').removeClass('glyphicon-chevron-right');
          return sidebar(2);
        } else {
          $('#toggleSidebar i').removeClass('glyphicon-chevron-left');
          $('#toggleSidebar i').addClass('glyphicon-chevron-right');
          return sidebar(1);
        }
      });
      function sidebar(panels) {
          $.asm.panels = panels;
          if (panels === 1) {
             $("body").removeClass("modal-open");
             $('#sidebar-content').css('overflow-y','hidden');
             $('#sidebar').animate({//hide
                  left: -($('#sidebar').width()+30),
            });
          } else if (panels === 2) {//show
             $("body").addClass("modal-open");
             $('#sidebar-content').css('overflow-y','scroll');
             $('#sidebar').animate({
                  left: 0,
              });
          }
      };
      $(document).mouseup(function (e){
        var container = $("#sidebar");
          if (!container.is(e.target)&& container.has(e.target).length === 0 && $('#toggleSidebar *').hasClass('glyphicon-chevron-left')){
            $('#toggleSidebar').trigger('click');
          }
      });
      $(window).on('resize load',function(){
        $('#sidebar-content').css('max-height',$(window).height()-50);
        if($('.glyphicon-chevron-right').length){
          $('#sidebar').css('left',-($('#sidebar').width()+30));
        }
      });
    </script>

        }
      }
</style>

<script>
        $('[data-toggle=popover]').popover({html:true,
          trigger:'manual'
        });
        $('[data-toggle=popover]').on('click',function(e){
          $(e.currentTarget).popover('toggle');
        });
        $('[data-toggle=popover]').on('focusout',function(e){
          setTimeout(function(){
                $(e.currentTarget).popover('toggle');
          },200);
        });
        var popover=$(".lightboxadd").data('bs.popover');
        $('.modal').find('img').css('max-height',$(window).height()*.7);
        function setmodal(arr){
            //{"columns":["imgnum","subid","commonname","scientificname","autid","photographer","org","baseimgurl","landscape","description"],"
            $('#modal').find('img').one("load", function() {
            }).attr("src",arr[7]+'768x512/'+arr[0]+'.jpg');
            $('.imglink').attr('href',$('.imglink').attr('href').replace(/=.*/,'='+arr[0]));
            $('.sublink').attr('href',$('.sublink').attr('href').replace(/=.*/,'='+arr[1]));
            $('.autlink').attr('href',$('.autlink').attr('href').replace(/=.*/,'='+arr[4]));
            if(typeof popover!="undefined"){
                $('[name=contentid]').val(arr[0]);
                var options='';
                $.ajax({
                    url: apiroot+'version/.json?contentid='+arr[0]+'&systemid=2',
                    success: function (response) {
                        for(var i=0;i<response.items.length;i++){
                            options+=getlightboxstring(response.items[i].id,response.items[i].text);
                        }
                        var maxversion = response.items.reduce(function(max, arr) {
                            return max >= arr.id ? max : arr.id;
                        }, -Infinity);
                       $('[data-target=".collectionmodal"]').data('versionid',maxversion);
                       $('[data-target=".collectionmodal"]').data('hide','[name=versionid]');
                        popover.options.content=options;
                    },
                    dataType: 'json'
                });
                function getlightboxstring(versionid,versionname){
                    return "  <button class='lightbox  btn btn-link' data-versionid='"+versionid+"' data-contentid='"+arr[0]+"' data-method='Lightbox.add' data-systemid='2' data-title='"+versionname+"'>"+versionname+" </button><br/>";
                }
                $('[data-target=".collectionmodal"]').data('contentid',$(this).data('id'));
                 $("[data-toggle=popover]").on('shown.bs.popover',function(){
                    Lightbox.setbuttons();
                    $('.lightbox').on('click',function(e){
                        eval($(this).data('method')+'($(this))');
                        e.relatedTarget.off();
                    });
                 });
            }
            $('#modal').modal('show');
            $('#modalcitation').html("Cite as: "+arr[arr.length-1]);
             $('#modal').find('.modal-title:first').html(('<strong>'+arr[3]+' (<em>'+arr[2].replace('spp.','sp.').trim()+'</em>)</strong> '+arr[9].toLowerCase()).replace(/\(\)/,''));  
        }
        $('#modal').on('shown.bs.modal', function (e) {
           var element=document.getElementById('modal');
            if (element.offsetHeight < element.scrollHeight) {
                 $('#modal').find('img').css("max-height",$('#modal').find('img').height()-(element.scrollHeight-element.offsetHeight));
            } 
        });
    </script>

<link href="/static/css/finitescroll.css" rel="stylesheet"/>
<script src="/static/js/finitescroll.js" type="text/javascript"></script>
<script type="text/javascript">
        jQuery(function($) {
             delete params['page'];
             delete params['start'];
             finite=$('#imagecontainer').finitescroll({
                        url:apiroot+'image/.json',
                        querystring:isUrban+'include=descriptor,dateupdated,citation&fmt=datatable&order[0][column]=0&order[0][dir]=desc&columns[8][searchable]=false&columns[1][searchable]=false&columns[7][searchable]=false&columns[10][searchable]=false&columns[4][searchable]=false&columns[11][searchable]=false',
                        totalcount:'#totalcount',
                        data:params,
                    });
             searchterm='';
             var timer;
             $(document).on('keyup','#sidebarsearch',function(e){
                var val = $(this).val();
                window.clearTimeout(timer);
                if( val !==searchterm || e.keyCode==17){
                    searchterm=val;
                    params['search[value]']=val;
                    timer = window.setTimeout(function(){
                        object.reload();
                    },800); 
                }
             });
             $('#searchform').submit(function(e){
                var val = $('#sidebarsearch').val();
                e.preventDefault();
                if( val !==searchterm){
                    searchterm=val;
                    params['search[value]']=val;
                }
                object.reload();
             })
            $(document).on('click','.item',function(){
                finite=finite.finitescroll('getimage',$(this).data('id'));
                setmodal($('#imagecontainer').data('finitescroll').openimage);
            });
        });
        object={
            reload:function(){
                $('#imagecontainer').finitescroll('redraw',params);
            }
        };
        i = 0;
    </script>
